  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">It pleases me to announce to you that our latest research paper here at the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Next4biz</a> R&amp;D Center, "Graph Based Business Process Anomaly Detection with Edge Feature Reconstruction and Advanced Linear Networks" is now available on IEEE Xplore through the link below.

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/gErg3wKa?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/gErg3wKa</a>

This study is part of an extensive research series conducted here at the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/next4biz?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Next4biz</a> R&amp;D Center under the project AnomalyNet, a state-of-the-art business process anomaly detection framework aiming to help business users with their process inefficiencies.

Our study, presented at the 7th International Congress on Human-Computer Interaction, Optimization and Robotic Applications (ICHORA), is a continuation of a previous study presented at the International Computer Engineering Conference (UBMK). It expands upon its predecessor with a more informative graph construction scheme and a more complex neural network architecture.

If you wish to learn more about the software solutions developed here, feel free to check out our paper.</p>
